Lily can run 12 kilometers per hour for 4 hours, so she runs 12 kilometers per hour x 4 hours = 48 kilometers.
After that, she runs 6 kilometers per hour for the remaining 4 hours, so she runs 6 kilometers per hour x 4 hours = 24 kilometers.
In total, Lily runs 48 kilometers + 24 kilometers = 72 kilometers in 8 hours.
Therefore, the value is 72
